	</div>
	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" >Wikidata:WikiProject Freebase/Mapping</h1>
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikidata</div>
		<div id="contentSub"><span class="subpages">&lt; <a href="/wiki/Wikidata:WikiProject_Freebase" title="Wikidata:WikiProject Freebase">Wikidata:WikiProject Freebase</a></span></div>
		<div id="contentSub2"></div>
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p>The goal of this page is to build a mapping from Freebase properties to Wikidata ones in order to feed the <a href="/wiki/Wikidata:Primary_sources_tool" title="Wikidata:Primary sources tool">Primary Sources tool</a>.
</p><p>To map a Freebase property to a Wikidata property, one just appends it with the property number using the <a href="/wiki/Template:P" class="mw-redirect" title="Template:P">P template</a>. If the property can not be mapped to an existing Wikidata property and is the reverse of another one that is already mapped to Wikidata or is not really relevant to Wikidata, just remove it. If you think the property is relevant to be added to Wikidata, you could create a <a href="/wiki/Wikidata:Property_proposal" title="Wikidata:Property proposal">property proposal</a> and add a link to it. 
</p><p>Example:
</p>
<pre>* https://www.freebase.com/people/person/date_of_birth {{p|569}}</pre>
<p>That gives:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="https://www.freebase.com/people/person/date_of_birth">https://www.freebase.com/people/person/date_of_birth</a> <a href="/wiki/Property:P569" title="Property:P569">date of birth&#32;<small dir="ltr">(P569)</small></a></li></ul>
<p>The main discussion page for this project is: <a href="/wiki/Wikidata_talk:WikiProject_Freebase" title="Wikidata talk:WikiProject Freebase">Wikidata talk:WikiProject Freebase</a>.
</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3">3</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikidata:WikiProject_Freebase/Mapping&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 3">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th>Freebase property
</th>
<th>Wikidata property
</th>
<th>Comments
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="3">Freebase Schemastaging was an area for work-in-progress schema that had not been officially promoted to /commons. The schema here was influx and under constant revision by Google and the Experts community until it was promoted to /commons. Recommended not to import, but perhaps to use as a basis for creating New properties that Wikidata might like to have.
</td></tr>

		<ul class="vector-menu-content-list"></ul>
